5a1(1): tsU hU~M hUM/ de nas yab yum gnyis su med pa las/ khro bo dang khro mo dang / sprul pa dang / yang sbrul du bcas po tha nga cod thon par gyur nas/ hUM hU~M hU~M/ 
5a2(1): pa Ta phaT paT badz+ra ki la ya hUM phaT/ ces pa rdo rje phur pa drag po'i sgra nas/ 'jig rten dregs pa'i rba songs nas/ yang rang bzhin gyi sa gnyis su med par mnyam pa nyid kyis bzhugs
5a3(1): te/ sbya ra lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bzhugs so// rdo rje khros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ gleng bsnang ba'i le'u ste/ gnyis pa'o// 
5a4(1): / de ltar mnyam pa nyid la gnas pa la/ bdag tu rmongs pa dang / rtags pa la mngon par zhen pa'i dbang gis/ yang dag pa'i lam dang bral
5a5(1): nas/ gab pa'i gsang ba ni ma rtogs par/ sbas pas gsang ba la mngon par bzhen nas/ rgyu dang 'bras bu la rmongs nas/ srid pa'i sa bon gtsub mor gyur pa nas/ 
5a6(1): ba'i dmyal bar skyes so// tsha ba'i sdug bsngal gyis brdungs pas// shin tu grang ba'i nang du skyes/ tsha ba dang grang ba dang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyud cing / bskal pa stong
5a7(1): phrag bcu gnyis su myong ngo // de nas yan lag sna tshogs pa dang / gdug pa'i lag cha sna tshogs pa dang / nad bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi 'debs par byed la/ lha'i rigs dang lha
5a8(1): ma yin da / tshangs pa dang 'bras bu che ba man chad dbang du bsdus so// bde bar gshegs pa thams cad mkhyen pas gzigs nas/ thugs rje gyis brlabs kyis// 
5b1(1): bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyis sras su bskyed nas/ 
5b2(1): sras ni chos nyid skye ba med pa las// 'jigs pa'i gzugs skur bzhengs pa'i phyir na sras// mchog ni de las bzhengs kyang g.yo' ba med// sras ni ru Ta 'dul phyir mi bzad pur
5b3(1): pa drug/ ces bde bar gshegs byin gyis brlabs kyi nas// dbu gsum phyag zhabs sprul pa'i phra men ma/ byi la'i 'gro can dang / phug shud kyi 'go can no// oM badz+ra kro ta a pa ra tsi ta trAM/ 
5b4(1): tista ti swa hU~M phaT/ nung byang du khro bo chen po gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / yum rdo rje mda' bsnyems ma/ sprul pa phra men ma/ spyang ku'i mgo can/ wa'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro ta a myi
5b5(1): ta kun d+ha liM hUM/ tshin d+ha tshin d+ha hUM phaT/ byang du khro bo chen po bdud rtsi 'khyil ba dang / sprul pa'i phra men ma seng ge'i mgo can dang / pa wang gi mgo can no// A~M badz+ra kro ha tre'i lo kya'i 6
5b6(1): ya hUM/ bin d+ha bin d+ha hUM phaT/ byang shar du khro bo rnam par rgyal ba dang / yum rdo rje gsod byed ma chen mo/ sprul pa'i phra man ma tred kyi mgo can dang / sre mo'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra/ 
5b7(1): kro ta ma hA pa la hUM phaT/ s+pho te s+pho te hUM phaT/ 'og tu khro bo stobs po che dang / yum rdo rje bstong byed ma/ sprul pa'i phra men dom gyi mgo can dang / byi ba'i mgo can gyis gtams
5b8(1): pa'o// de rnams thams cad kyang thon par gyur te/ rab tu khros par gyur to// oM badz+ra ki li ki la ya hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ ces rab rgya mkhos te/ stong gsum dus gcig
6a1(1): g.yos so// srin po chen po gdug pa dang bcas pa bris so// mi thub par 'chor ba las bkyim ldan pa nga rdo rje gzhon nu nyid kyis/ shin
6a2(1): tu khros rab tu 'khros pa las/ mi bzod pa'i sras mchog rnam pa drug mthon par gyur te/ ta pra ya ta tha ya hUM phaT/ ha sa ya ha na hUM phaT/ shi kri na ha na hUM phaT/ bi da ya
6a3(1): bi da ya hUM phaT/ ces sras mchog rnam pa drug gis/ rlong chen drug gis las bya ste// stod ni zhal gsum phyag drug pa// smad ni zur gsum dpal dang ldan// khro bo
6a4(1): bcu yis yongs brgyan nas// bdug par lus 'dul bar byos// snying rjes bsgral bas dam tshig ni// gsod cing mnan pa ma yin te// phung por rdo rje rnams byas nas/ 
6a5(1): rnam par shes pa rdo rjer bsgom// hUM hUM hUM ki li ki la ya ces rab tu 'azos pas/ rang dbang chen por bskur te/ rdo rje gzhon nus rigs rnams// srid pa rdo rje grub mdzod cig
6a6(1): srid pa rdo rje bung pa'i lnga/ ye shes khri grub par mdzod// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes sku// nga nyid rdo rje chos dbyings las// 'bar nga'i bzhi pa gcig tu sprul nas/ 
6a7(1): hUMhU~M/ baT ba Ta phaT/ ces 'bros lus po cig la mgo brgyad par sprul/ phyag na mtshan cha sna tshogs bsnams pa/ 'khor thams cad kyang bsdus nas/ shin tu
6a8(1): 'gyir bag dang bcas par gyur to// hi hi hi zhes shi na nga rgyal dang bcas par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das sras mchog nyid kyis/ dur khrod kyi rlo rin gdug pa can gyi gdang
6b1(1): la bzhugs nas/ A~M ki li ki la la sarba big nan hUM phaT/ ces brjod pas rngam brjid dang ldan par gyur to// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing ba/ nal gsum
6b2(1): mche ba bcu gnyis pa/ shangs gsum pa bsdu gyen du 'khyil ba/ phyag drug dang pon rdo rje rtse dgupa/ ba pa rje lnga pa/ g.yon gyi dang pon me dpung / bar ba na khaT rtse gsum pa/ 
6b3(1): tha ma gnyis kyis rdo rje phur pa 'gril ba/ dur khrod kyi chas brgyad gsol ba/ rdzu 'phrul gyi zhabs bzhis bzhugs pa/ rdo rje gshog pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams khengs pa/ sku mchog
6b4(1): gang ba'i lus la gtams pa/ yum dang gnyis su med par gyur to// / rdo rje 'khros pa zhe sdang gcod// mtshon cha sngon po 'bar ba yis// na mkha'i dkyil
6b5(1): nas thigs pa shar// srog gi go ru shar pa dang / snying gi gau ru bsgom par bya/ ces gsungs so// de nas khro bo'i tshogs thams cad sprul pa las/ 
6b6(1): A~M badz+ra kro ha hU~M kar gar dza gar dza hU~M phaT/ ces steng du khro bo chen po hU~M kar/ yum rdo rje sgra 'byin ma/ sbal pa'i 'phra men ma/ bag gi 'go can dang / smig bu'i mgo can no// A~M
6b7(1): kro ta bi dza ya hUM/ he na ha na hUM phaT/ shar du khro bo chen po rnam par rgyal ba dang / yum rdo rje rnam par bsnyems ma/ sprul pa'i 'dra men ma/ stag gi mgo can dang / bya rgod kyi 'gro
6b8(1): can no// A~M kro ta ni la ha na tha hUM phaT/ d+ha ha d+ha ha hUM phaT/ shar lho'i mtshams su khro bo chen po dbyug pa sngon po can dang / yum rdo rje skyer mo la/ sprul pa'i 'phra men ma/ 
8a1(1): sha zos khrag 'chos rus pa kun 'chos nas/ hUM hUM hU~M phaT phaT phaT/ ces brjod pa bden pa'i don ras su 'chi 'badas su 'chi/ 
8a2(1): 'bangs su mchil nan ha na ma tshungs cig/ shes pa bla myed gnas stabs nas// phung po dur khrod gnas bya zhing / gzugs phung nga'i gdan bya'o// chos nyid kyi bden pa'o// 
8a3(1): gsang sngags kyis byin gyis brlabs so// sangs kyi mthu'o// a bi ra tsa'i dus la bab po// gnag pa de kho na la'o// ces byin gyis brlabs kyis snang ngo // rdo rje 'gro
8a4(1): pa rtse brgyad las/ drag pa drags pa can gtul ba'i le'u sa gsum pa'o// / de nas dregs pa 'dul ba'i rtse bo// 'jig
8a5(1): rten gyi dregs pa po mo rnams spangs nas/ ye shes dang las la grub pa'i bud myed dkar mo shel gyi lan phran can gyis kyang / srog gi snying po phul nas/ dpa' bo chen po/ 
8a6(1): 'khor bcas la// bdag cag rnams kyang 'bangs su mchi// yang bud med nag mo khrag gi ral pa can gyis kyang / bdag gi srog gi snying po bzhengs su gsol// de yang bu
8a7(1): myed dmar mo byi ru'i rdang ral can gyis/ dpa' bo chen po'i spyan lam du// bdag gi srog sring dam pa 'di/ dpa' bo khyod kyi bzhes su gsol// a tsi ha a pa ran
8a8(1): he/ dza ya bing ye/ ka ta~M ka he ye/ mar san bla mar na ni ye hU~M phaT/ bdag cag rnams kyi srog snying 'di// dpa' bo chen pos bzhes su gsol// sku gsung thugs
8b1(1): las rdzogs bsngags/ dpa' bo khyod la 'bul bar bgyi/ ces srog gis snying po phul nas/ khas blangs dam bcas las/ rdo rje gsang ba'i bka' las ni/ sdig
8b2(1): gang zhig 'da' byed pa// khro chen khro bo chen po yis// glad pa tshal ba brgya ru khos// nyon cig bgegs dang log 'dren tshogs// nga yi bka' las 'da' ma byed// ces gan/ 
8b3(1): 'al bor bas/ yang srog gi snying po phul te// dpa' bo thugs kyi dkyil 'khor du// bdag cag 'khor dang bcas pa yi// srog gi snying po 'bul bar bgyi// bka'i pha
8b4(1): 'bag gsal du gsol// bruM ma ma nga shing ku ru/ ma taM nya kar a nan/ r+ha ti ma ma kar ma/ shi kr-i ka re ya hU~M phaT/ dpa' bo chen po'i spyan lam du// sreg snying drag sngags
8b5(1): 'di dbul gyis// thugs rje spyan gyis gzigs su gsol// ces phul lo// 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// 'khor 'das bcas pa ma kun// dam chos 'di la
8b6(1): brten pa yis// ma lus las rnam grub par gyis// dam tshig chen po'i dus la bab// sprul pa chen po'i dus la bab// bdag nyid chen mo'i dus la bab// sho na mu kha'i
8b7(1): dus la bab/ sa bdag chen mo'i dus la ba/ khyod kyi thugs dam dus la bab// mthu rtsal byung ba'i dus la bab// ces nad la bor nas dam rdzas la brten cing bran gyi/ 
8b8(1): tshul du khas blangs so// ston pa chen po sangs rgyas gtso// drag po chen po 'jigs pa'i gzugs// mnyam pa srid kyi mcho mardo rlig/ zhi ba'i sems can
10a1(1): pa dang / sdug bsngal bskyed pa la sogs bya// rdungs cig rdo rje 'bar ba'i brtun// bka' las 'da' byad rdo rje me dpal snying bsregs
10a2(1): nas// lus ngag rdul phran bzhin du grogs// khro mo 'bar ba'i rtun khung du// rdo rje tho ba'i brdung bar bya// lha yang rung ste brlag par 'gyur// kha tha ma kha tha ma kha tham pa Ta phaT paT/ 
10a3(1): badz+ra yag sha kr-i ta kha hi kha hi/ ha ha ha/ yangab yum bar du brdung bya zhing // dngos po sha khrag lha yis sku// stabs pa'i dgyes pas rta rgad 'gyur// nyi shu rtsa gcig sngags rnams kyis/ 
10a4(1): dkar nag 'tshams su gdab par bya// hUM hUM hUM phaT pa TaT/ rdo rje bakhros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ dgegs btul ba'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// 
10a5(1): de nas mnyam pa'i ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs nas/ dmyigs pa byed pa'i ting nge 'dzin 'dis/ ting nge 'dzin rgyal por bstan par gyur// ma nor ma bcos dbyings nyid las// rang bzhin
10a6(1): lhun gyis grub pa'i dbyings// dngos myed gsal ba'i ye shes la// de la sems kyi 'bras bu bskyed// thog mar gzhan yang byang chub sems// de ni rgyu 'bras ma bkag chos// 
10a7(1): de nas bdag gi byang chub sems// srid pa gsum la dbang bsgyur zhing / bag ban dang skal pa gcig/ byang chub sems ni mngon du bstan/ khams sems na mngan de bas na// khams
10a8(1): gsum ye shes bskyed pa'i phyir// bsgrub pa'i ye shes mtshon gang po// gsad pa'i sngags kyi bskyed nas kyang // sku dang ldan par rab brgyan cing // khams gsum khro bos gang bar mdzod// 
10b1(1): gnyis ldan sku gsung thugs su ldan// shin tu brjid pa'i ye shes kyis// sku'i tshig gis rab brgyan cing // thugs la 'bar ba'i srog kyang bzhugs// dbu la rdzogs pa'i rigs lnga
10b2(1): bsrung // he zla'i ri rab phur bur brgyan// khro ba mang po bzir mnan nas// yum ni rnam par grol ba'i thugs// srid pa'i phur bu rtogs pa'i ngang // srid pa gsum yang thebs zhes bya/ 
10b3(1): khams gsum gdul bsngal ba'i phyir// mtshan ma gzi brjid glog ltar 'bar// me dpung gsum gyis khams gsum bsreg/ nyes byed gsum yang srid par bsnol// khams gsum
10b4(1): dus gcig dbang bskur nas// rab tu srog gi gor shar ba// gnyis ldan sku gsung thugs su ldan// dus cig leb 'bar bar smin// rdzogs na dud kha gsang phyir ro// mthil la gnyis
10b5(1): zla'i dkyil 'khor bsgom// lag tu blangs te dril nas kyang // khams gsum du kha bsgral gyur// yum bzhi phyag rgya'i byin rlabs zhing // de nas a las rnam par dag/ srid pa gsuM
10b6(1): du gsal 'tsher nas// 'khor ba gsum ni mya ngan 'das// 'di ni byang chub sems kyi 'khrus// byang chub sems kyi khyad par las// khro bo'i phur bu'i rab brgyan cig/ khams
10b7(1): gsum dbang bar yang dag grub// des na yul sems gnyis su med// skye ba myed pa'i don rab gyis// kha'i rtun khung bde gshegs gnas// gting dpag myed pa'i dbyings nyid
10b8(1): du// lha yang rung ste myos brgyal nas// srid pa'i phur bu thebs zhes bya// zo mo 'bar ba'i rtun khung du// khro bo 'bar ba'i tan rtogs kyi ma byang chub sems kyi 'phro 'dra yis// 
11a1(1): khams gsum ma lus bsgral zhes bya// rnam par shes pa ye shes mchog/ srog dang rmugs/ byang chub sems kyi phur pa
11a2(1): las// mkhas pa bzhin du lhun gyis grub// mnyam pa'i rgyal pos yang dag bskal// rtog 'dzin med pa'i dbang brag des// dpa' bo chen po 'dul ba bzhin// shin tu bsngal te
11a3(1): dgyes btab nas/ za byed kun gyis stobs par mdzod// ha ha ba gyes pas dgyes par mdzod// phaT phaT kyis ni 'khor lo bri// hUM hU~M bgyis dbang du bsdud// kha hi bgyis lhag ma
11a4(1): bzhes// rdo rje rab tu ki la ya// rab tu gsor te dril nas kyang // khams gsum 'khor bar bsgral bar bya// sems yul rnams bsgral nas ni// ye shes sku'i khyab brdal nas/ 
11a5(1): 'dzin chags thams cad rnam par grol// de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu// byang chub sems las 'od 'phros pas// mkhas pa de bzhin rol pa'i sku// ma lus phur bu thebs zhes bya/ 
11a6(1): gang zhig gnas pa'i phyogs rnams la// rnam par shes pa'i tshogs brgyad gnas// rdo rje phur pa ma shar shing // de'i tshogs brgyad dag par bya// bdag dang gsum du ldan nas kyang / 
11a7(1): byang chub sems la dbang smos te// phung po rdul du bzhig nas kyang // sha zag khams gsum gang bar dmigs// bruM gis rab tu nam mkha' gang // par kyis kun tu gtor bya ste// rdo rje
11a8(1): yeshem mtshan gang gis/ khams gsum rab tu bged nas kyang // solas rab tu dag pa yis// sring po 'di skad ces 'arjod do// rab tung mchog sems rab tugasal ba'i phyi
11b1(1): mtsham yin rig rgyal las rang ci tshul// de bzhin tshugs drangs nas ni// phung po ga'isun ba nas kyang // bsdus pa'i mig la chen por bsgom// khams gsum byang chub sems brtsa/ 
11b2(1): / 'gro ba ma lus don pa'i phyir// spos pa ljang kun nam mkha' khyab// dmar po srog gi thugs kyang lags// ljang kun las kyi sa bon te// mthing ka he ru ka'i thugs/ 
11b3(1): thams cad kun tu brjod 'grub pas// de nges sems kyi phung po 'tshal// khams gsum dur khrod khrag yin te// thugs rjes chags pa bsgral ba'i phyir// srid pa brdar sha bcad nas ni/ 
11b4(1): spyod pa rnams bcud dang ldan// hU~M zhes bya ba skal bzang ngo // srid pa dbang du bsdus nas ni// khams gsum kun las 'das par bsgom// 'jig rten kun las 'das par bsgom// 'jig rten
11b5(1): kun las 'das pas na// ldan na po dang bdag nyid sbyor// 'jig rten kun las grub pa'i rgyal// man ngag nyid khu gsang ba'i rjes// 'dzin dang rtog pa rnam spangs te// byang chub sems
11b6(1): ni skad cig mu// snang dang srid dang 'dzin rtog dang // bsam pa las 'das mya ngan 'das// 'jig rten pa las mya ngan 'das// byang chub sems kyi grolas gcad// grub mtha' 'di la
11b7(1): 'jig mtha' myed// 'di ni myi 'gyur byang chub sems// mya ngan 'das pa rtogs pa mo// sgrib pa med pa mtha' byin pa// byas pa myed par lhun gyis grub// myi nus pa la rtog byas shing / 
11b8(1): 'arje sems dpa'i rnam 'a lanub// nub med pa zhin tu spags// 'di ni kun gyi phra gnas// sman gyi zu gar gsang ba yin/ mchi chi rjed ban// byang chub sems ni rdzogs
12a1(1): so nas// man ngag cing lugs ba'i rdzas// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor cing bskul la// ma dzad panyer du bzhag par mdzod// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
12a2(1): cad la// bstan pa'i snying po de la med// man ngag bstan pa'i snying po 'di// don gyi bcu dpyangs sangs rgyas // 'di las gzhan zhes bya bar ni// sangs rgyas nyid kyi mi mkhyen no// 
12a3(1): rdo rje 'khros pa rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ ting nge 'dzin bstan la dbab pa'i le'u ste drag pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje
12a4(1): gzhon nyid kyis gdug pa can thams cad dus cig tu 'dul ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dur khrod chen po'i klong na/ dur khrod kyi gzhal yas khang // me lha drang srong bsreg pa'i
12a5(1): mchog/ lho nub srin po nan pa'i gnas// byang chub rlung lha 'phang dang dbye ba ste// byang shar 'byung po dbang ldan sgrol la mkhas// dkyil 'khor po zang myi 'gyur brtan pa'i mchog
12a6(1): gdug pa can gyi mthu phrog phyir// bsnyen bsgrub gnyis kyi las bya'o// bkra shis byin brlabs yod pa'i phyir// skad cig pa 'am skad gnyis pa// gnod par shes pa'i sa de ru// 
12a7(1): phyogs skyong bcu dang rgyal chen bzhi// bsrung ba'i rim pa'i tshul bzhin bya// ma 'da' 'dom gang grub bzhi la// gong du smos pa bzhin du bri// ma tang khong par gnas bcas nas// 
12a8(1): skye med thabs dbyings phur pa ni// mnyam nyid skye ba med pas thebs// thugs rje phur pa'i thugs rje yis// log par 'khyams pa rnams la gdab// gsang ba'i byang chub sem
12b1(1): kyi bung ba 'di// rtogs chags 'dul ba'i phyir yum gyi mkha' la brdab// 'dus byas rdzas kyi bur pa 'dis// bskal ba'i zhing bcur gyur pa rnams la gdab// 'dus byas rdzas
12b2(1): kyi bur pa la// man ngag nyid du bkod pa bdun// med du mi rung de bzhin bsam snyan pur rnam pa gnyis yin te// nyungs kar dang ni phrar bu dngos// lcags sna lnga 'am bdun kyang rung / 
12b3(1): 'gro brgya mdung rtse zur gsum pa// rkyed pargya mdud bzhal yas khang // khyim pa zhog brgyad la sor bcu gnyis// spen pa'i bur par de bzhin bya// seng ldeng bur bu sor brgyad ni/ 
12b4(1): mthu 'phrog byin brlabs yod pa yin// de bzhin bya rgod gshog pur yang // 'gugs par byed pa'i nus pa yod// ser po gser ram yang na ni// ster ba dag la byas pa yis/ 
12b5(1): zil gyis mnan pa'i phur ba yin// skyes pa dang ma'i rigs can gyi// sdom pa ma yin 'phra mo 'am// rangs sam ljon dmar shing dag gam// dmar po dag la byas pa 'di/ 
12b6(1): dbang du bsdud pas bung ba bstan// tsan dan dag gam rgya shug gi/ gzi byin 'phrog par yang dag bstan// lcags sam shi shing nag po 'am// drag por gyur pa mtha' dag la/ 
12b7(1): gdul du klog par rab tu bstan// phyogs kyi khro bo bcu po la// bcu mtshan bcu 'am yang na bcu na bcu// de bzhin mang nyung grangs kyis dbye// mthing nag dar gyi gcod paN gdags/ 
12b8(1): lha 'am rdzas su spyod kyang rung // mtshan dang ldan pa'i ban da ru// nag po 'bru yi bkang nas ni// rim par shugs shing byin gyis brlabs// mthing nag dar gyi kha gcad nas/ 
13a1(1): byin brlabs dbang bskur gzhung bzhin bya// mi 'gyur po breb rdzas su bkod// re lda rnam pa'o saur// drag po'i sgom thab
13a2(1): bzhung bzhin bya// tsher ma can gyi shing btsugs la// ming dang rus su bcas pa dang // drag po rtsang gis bskor bar bya// bsreg pa'i rdzas rnams kun kyang bzhag/ rtswa
13a3(1): nub srin po mnan pa'i sar// de bzhin drag po gru gsum la// rim pa gsum du bskor// mon nam rabs chad thod pa la// gang yin ming rus bris nas ni// mtha' ma drag po'i
13a4(1): rtsang gis bskor// gru gsum dbus kyi steng du gzhag/ log pa med pa mthar phyin pa'i// brgya dang brgyad kyis phur pas bskor// mtha' ma de bzhin rtsang gis bskor/ 
13a5(1): byang nub rlung lha 'phang dbye ba'i sar// drag po gru gsum gong bzhin bya// thod pa dum bu drug pa 'am// mtshan ma ngan par gyur pa yis// bri ba'i thabs ni gang yin bri// gang yin
13a6(1): ming rus bcu bcug nas ni// drag po gru gsum dbus su bzhag/ man ngag nyid du bkod pa yi// bur bu zur gsum dpal dang ldan// drag po'i gtor ma steng du bkod// khrag sna lnga dang / 
13a7(1): snying sna lnga// mtshan ga nyungs nas mda'// drag po zer gyi rdzas su bzhag/ mtha' ma de bzhin rtsang gis bskor// byang shar 'byung po dbang ldan sgrol ba'i sar// gru gsum rim
